-- ----------------------------
-- Table structure for approval_cc_users
-- ----------------------------
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `approval_cc_users`;
CREATE TABLE `approval_cc_users`  (
  `id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `instance_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'е®Ўжү№е®һдҫӢID',
  `user_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'жҠ„йҖҒдәәID',
  `user_name` varchar(100) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'жҠ„йҖҒдәәе§“еҗҚ',
  `added_by` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'ж·»еҠ дәәID',
  `added_at_step` tinyint(0) NOT NULL COMMENT 'еңЁе“ӘдёӘжӯҘйӘӨж·»еҠ зҡ„',
  `has_read` tinyint(1) NULL DEFAULT 0 COMMENT 'жҳҜеҗҰе·ІиҜ»',
  `read_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'йҳ…иҜ»ж—¶й—ҙ',
  `created_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(0),
  `updated_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_instance`(`instance_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_user`(`user_id`, `has_read`) USING BTREE
) ENGINE = InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT = 5 CHARACTER SET = utf8mb4 COLLATE = utf8mb4_unicode_ci COMMENT = 'е®Ўжү№жҠ„йҖҒиЎЁ' ROW_FORMAT = Compact;

-- ----------------------------
-- Table structure for approval_instances

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `approval_instances`;
CREATE TABLE `approval_instances`  (
  `id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `account_set_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'иҙҰеҘ—ID',
  `business_type` varchar(50) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'дёҡеҠЎзұ»еһӢпјҡemployee_contract, salary, insuranceзӯү',
  `business_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'дёҡеҠЎж•°жҚ®ID',
  `current_step` tinyint(0) NOT NULL DEFAULT 1 COMMENT 'еҪ“еүҚе®Ўжү№жӯҘйӘӨ',
  `total_steps` tinyint(0) NOT NULL DEFAULT 4 COMMENT 'жҖ»е®Ўжү№жӯҘйӘӨж•°',
  `status` enum('pending','approved','rejected','cancelled') CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'pending' COMMENT 'ж•ҙдҪ“зҠ¶жҖҒ',
  `created_by` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'еҸ‘иө·дәәID',
  `attachment_path` varchar(500) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'йҷ„д»¶и·Ҝеҫ„пјҲеҗҲеҗҢж–Үд»¶зӯүпјү',
  `attachment_name` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'йҷ„д»¶еҺҹе§Ӣж–Үд»¶еҗҚ',
  `created_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(0),
  `updated_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(0) ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(0),
  `completed_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'е®ҢжҲҗж—¶й—ҙ',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_account_business`(`account_set_id`, `business_type`, `business_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_status`(`status`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_created_by`(`created_by`) USING BTREE
) ENGINE = InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT = 202 CHARACTER SET = utf8mb4 COLLATE = utf8mb4_unicode_ci COMMENT = 'е®Ўжү№жөҒзЁӢе®һдҫӢиЎЁ' ROW_FORMAT = Compact;

-- ----------------------------
-- Table structure for approval_records
-- ----------------------------
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `approval_records`;
CREATE TABLE `approval_records`  (
  `id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `instance_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'е®Ўжү№е®һдҫӢID',
  `step_order` tinyint(0) NOT NULL COMMENT 'е®Ўжү№жӯҘйӘӨпјҡ1,2,3,4',
  `step_name` varchar(50) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'жӯҘйӘӨеҗҚз§°пјҡз»ҸеҠһгҖҒеӨҚж ёгҖҒе®Ўж ёгҖҒз»Ҳе®Ў',
  `approver_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'е®Ўжү№дәәID',
  `approver_name` varchar(100) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'е®Ўжү№дәәе§“еҗҚ',
  `status` enum('waiting','pending','approved','rejected','returned') CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'waiting' COMMENT 'зҠ¶жҖҒпјҡwaiting=зӯүеҫ…дёӯ, pending=е®Ўжү№дёӯ, approved=е·ІйҖҡиҝҮ, rejected=е·Ій©іеӣһ, returned=е·ІйҖҖеӣһ',
  `comment` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL COMMENT 'е®Ўжү№ж„Ҹи§Ғ',
  `signature_image` varchar(500) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'зӯҫеҗҚеӣҫзүҮи·Ҝеҫ„',
  `seal_image` varchar(500) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'еҚ°з« еӣҫзүҮи·Ҝеҫ„',
  `returned_to_step` tinyint(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'йҖҖеӣһеҲ°зҡ„жӯҘйӘӨ',
  `returned_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'йҖҖеӣһж—¶й—ҙ',

-- Table structure for approvals

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `approvals`;
CREATE TABLE `approvals`  (
  `id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `account_set_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'жүҖеұһиҙҰеҘ—ID',
  `user_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `project_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `type` enum('leave','overtime','business_trip','expense','other') CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `title` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `content` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `start_date` date NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `end_date` date NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `amount` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT 0.00,
  `status` enum('pending','approved','rejected','returned') CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT 'pending',
  `comment` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL COMMENT 'е®Ўжү№ж„Ҹи§Ғ',
  `attachments` longtext CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_bin NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(0),
  `updated_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(0) ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(0),
  `approver_id` bigint(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `approved_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `rejected_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `submitted_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `actual_completion_date` date NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `related_id` bigint(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'дёҡеҠЎе…іиҒ”id',
  `applicant_id` bigint(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `reason` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `expected_completion_date` datetime(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `approval_comment` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `signature` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `seal` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `stamp_method` enum('online','offline') CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT 'online' COMMENT 'зӣ–з« ж–№ејҸпјҡonline=зәҝдёҠзӣ–з« пјҢoffline=зәҝдёӢзӣ–з« ',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `user_id`(`user_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `project_id`(`project_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_approvals_status`(`status`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_approvals_account_set_id`(`account_set_id`) USING BTREE
) ENGINE = InnoDB CHARACTER SET = utf8mb4 COLLATE = utf8mb4_unicode_ci ROW_FORMAT = Compact;

  `id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `account_set_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'иҙҰеҘ—ID',
  `attendance_sheet_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'иҖғеӢӨиЎЁID',

  `project_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'йЎ№зӣ®ID',
  `date` date NOT NULL COMMENT 'иҖғеӢӨж—Ҙжңҹ',
  `day_of_month` int(0) NOT NULL COMMENT 'жңҲд»Ҫдёӯзҡ„з¬¬еҮ еӨ©',
  `status` enum('normal','late','early','absent','leave','off') CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'normal' COMMENT 'иҖғеӢӨзҠ¶жҖҒ',
  `check_in_time` time(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'дёҠзҸӯж—¶й—ҙ',
  `check_out_time` time(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'дёӢзҸӯж—¶й—ҙ',
  `work_hours` decimal(4, 2) NULL DEFAULT 8.00 COMMENT 'е·ҘдҪңж—¶й•ҝ',
  `overtime_hours` decimal(4, 2) NULL DEFAULT 0.00 COMMENT 'еҠ зҸӯж—¶й•ҝ',
  `notes` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL COMMENT 'еӨҮжіЁ',
  `created_by` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'еҲӣе»әдәәID',
  `created_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`) USING BTREE,
  UNIQUE INDEX `unique_sheet_employee_day`(`attendance_sheet_id`, `employee_id`, `day_of_month`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_account_set_id`(`account_set_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_attendance_sheet_id`(`attendance_sheet_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_employee_id`(`employee_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_project_id`(`project_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_date`(`date`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_status`(`status`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_created_by`(`created_by`) USING BTREE
) ENGINE = InnoDB CHARACTER SET = utf8mb4 COLLATE = utf8mb4_unicode_ci COMMENT = 'иҖғеӢӨи®°еҪ•' ROW_FORMAT = Compact;

-- Table structure for attendance_rules
-- ----------------------------
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `attendance_rules`;
CREATE TABLE `attendance_rules`  (
  `id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `account_set_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'иҙҰеҘ—ID',
  `project_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'йЎ№зӣ®ID',
  `rule_name` varchar(100) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'и§„еҲҷеҗҚз§°',
  `work_start_time` time(0) NOT NULL DEFAULT '09:00:00' COMMENT 'дёҠзҸӯж—¶й—ҙ',
  `work_end_time` time(0) NOT NULL DEFAULT '18:00:00' COMMENT 'дёӢзҸӯж—¶й—ҙ',
  `late_threshold` int(0) NOT NULL DEFAULT 15 COMMENT 'иҝҹеҲ°йҳҲеҖј(еҲҶй’ҹ)',
  `early_threshold` int(0) NOT NULL DEFAULT 15 COMMENT 'ж—©йҖҖйҳҲеҖј(еҲҶй’ҹ)',
  `work_days_per_week` int(0) NOT NULL DEFAULT 5 COMMENT 'жҜҸе‘Ёе·ҘдҪңеӨ©ж•°',
  `is_active` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 1 COMMENT 'жҳҜеҗҰеҗҜз”Ё',
  `created_by` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'еҲӣе»әдәәID',
  `created_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_account_set_id`(`account_set_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_project_id`(`project_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_created_by`(`created_by`) USING BTREE
) ENGINE = InnoDB CHARACTER SET = utf8mb4 COLLATE = utf8mb4_unicode_ci COMMENT = 'иҖғеӢӨи§„еҲҷй…ҚзҪ®' ROW_FORMAT = Compact;

-- ----------------------------
-- Table structure for attendance_sheets
-- ----------------------------
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `attendance_sheets`;
CREATE TABLE `attendance_sheets`  (
  `id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `account_set_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'жүҖеұһиҙҰеҘ—ID',
  `project_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `month` varchar(7) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'жңҲд»Ҫ YYYY-MM',
  `work_days` int(0) NOT NULL DEFAULT 22 COMMENT 'е·ҘдҪңж—ҘеӨ©ж•°',
  `status` enum('draft','submitted','approved','rejected') CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT 'draft',
  `total_employees` int(0) NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `notes` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL COMMENT 'еӨҮжіЁ',
  `attachments` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL COMMENT 'жҸҗдәӨзҡ„йҷ„д»¶дҝЎжҒҜ(JSONж јејҸ)',
  `created_by` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'еҲӣе»әдәәID',
  `submitted_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `approved_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(0),
  `updated_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(0) ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(0),
  `submitted_by` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'жҸҗдәӨдәәID',
  `approved_by` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'е®Ўжү№дәәID',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `project_id`(`project_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_project_id`(`project_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_status`(`status`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_month`(`month`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_created_at`(`created_at`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_attendance_sheets_account_set_id`(`account_set_id`) USING BTREE
) ENGINE = InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT = 25 CHARACTER SET = utf8mb4 COLLATE = utf8mb4_unicode_ci ROW_FORMAT = Compact;

-- ----------------------------
-- Table structure for attendance_statistics
-- ----------------------------
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `attendance_statistics`;
CREATE TABLE `attendance_statistics`  (
  `id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `account_set_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'иҙҰеҘ—ID',
  `attendance_sheet_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'иҖғеӢӨиЎЁID',
  `employee_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'е‘ҳе·ҘID',
  `project_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'йЎ№зӣ®ID',
  `work_days` int(0) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0 COMMENT 'еә”еҮәеӢӨеӨ©ж•°',
  `actual_work_days` int(0) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0 COMMENT 'е®һйҷ…еҮәеӢӨеӨ©ж•°',
  `absent_days` int(0) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0 COMMENT 'зјәеӢӨеӨ©ж•°',
  `late_count` int(0) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0 COMMENT 'иҝҹеҲ°ж¬Ўж•°',
  `early_count` int(0) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0 COMMENT 'ж—©йҖҖж¬Ўж•°',
  `leave_days` int(0) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0 COMMENT 'иҜ·еҒҮеӨ©ж•°',
  `off_days` int(0) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0 COMMENT 'и°ғдј‘еӨ©ж•°',
  `attendance_rate` decimal(5, 4) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0.0000 COMMENT 'еҮәеӢӨзҺҮ',
  `total_work_hours` decimal(6, 2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0.00 COMMENT 'жҖ»е·ҘдҪңж—¶й•ҝ',
  `total_overtime_hours` decimal(6, 2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0.00 COMMENT 'жҖ»еҠ зҸӯж—¶й•ҝ',
  `created_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`) USING BTREE,
  UNIQUE INDEX `unique_sheet_employee`(`attendance_sheet_id`, `employee_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_account_set_id`(`account_set_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_attendance_sheet_id`(`attendance_sheet_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_employee_id`(`employee_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_project_id`(`project_id`) USING BTREE
) ENGINE = InnoDB CHARACTER SET = utf8mb4 COLLATE = utf8mb4_unicode_ci COMMENT = 'иҖғеӢӨз»ҹи®Ў' ROW_FORMAT = Compact;

  `old_housing_fund_base` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'и°ғж•ҙеүҚе…¬з§ҜйҮ‘еҹәж•°',

  `new_housing_fund_base` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'и°ғж•ҙеҗҺе…¬з§ҜйҮ‘еҹәж•°',
  `new_large_medical_base` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'и°ғж•ҙеҗҺеӨ§йўқеҢ»з–—еҹәж•°пјҲйҖүеЎ«пјү',
  `effective_date` date NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'з»ҹдёҖз”ҹж•Ҳж—¶й—ҙпјҲж—§еӯ—ж®өпјҢе·Іеәҹејғпјү',
  `status` enum('pending','approved','applied','cancelled') CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'pending' COMMENT 'зҠ¶жҖҒпјҡеҫ…е®Ўжү№гҖҒе·Іе®Ўжү№гҖҒе·Із”ҹж•ҲгҖҒе·ІеҸ–ж¶Ҳ',
  `applied_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'з”ҹж•Ҳж—¶й—ҙпјҲе®һйҷ…еә”з”ЁеҲ°жЎЈжЎҲзҡ„ж—¶й—ҙпјү',
  `adjustment_reason` varchar(500) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'и°ғж•ҙеҺҹеӣ ',
  `reason` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL COMMENT 'и°ғж•ҙеҺҹеӣ ',
  `remark` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL COMMENT 'еӨҮжіЁ',
  `approved_by` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'е®Ўжү№дәәID',
  `approved_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'е®Ўжү№ж—¶й—ҙ',
  `created_by` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'еҲӣе»әдәәID',
  `created_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(0),
  `updated_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(0) ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(0),
  `social_security_effective_date` date NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'зӨҫдҝқеҹәж•°з”ҹж•Ҳж—¶й—ҙ',
  `medical_insurance_effective_date` date NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'еҢ»дҝқеҹәж•°з”ҹж•Ҳж—¶й—ҙ',
  `housing_fund_effective_date` date NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'е…¬з§ҜйҮ‘еҹәж•°з”ҹж•Ҳж—¶й—ҙ',
  `large_medical_effective_date` date NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'еӨ§йўқеҢ»з–—еҹәж•°з”ҹж•Ҳж—¶й—ҙ',
  `social_security_min_base` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'зӨҫдҝқдёӢйҷҗпјҲи°ғеҹәж—¶пјү',
  `social_security_max_base` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'зӨҫдҝқдёҠйҷҗпјҲи°ғеҹәж—¶пјү',
  `medical_insurance_min_base` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'еҢ»дҝқдёӢйҷҗпјҲи°ғеҹәж—¶пјү',
  `medical_insurance_max_base` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'еҢ»дҝқдёҠйҷҗпјҲи°ғеҹәж—¶пјү',
  `housing_fund_min_base` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'е…¬з§ҜйҮ‘дёӢйҷҗпјҲи°ғеҹәж—¶пјү',
  `housing_fund_max_base` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'е…¬з§ҜйҮ‘дёҠйҷҗпјҲи°ғеҹәж—¶пјү',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_employee_id`(`employee_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_project_id`(`project_id`) USING BTREE,

  INDEX `idx_social_effective_date`(`social_security_effective_date`) USING BTREE

-- Table structure for bid_projects

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `bid_projects`;
CREATE TABLE `bid_projects`  (
  `id` int(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'йЎ№зӣ®ID',
  `account_set_id` int(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'иҙҰеҘ—ID',
  `project_code` varchar(50) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'йЎ№зӣ®зј–еҸ·пјҲиҮӘеҠЁз”ҹжҲҗпјү',
  `project_name` varchar(200) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'йЎ№зӣ®еҗҚз§°',
  `project_category` varchar(50) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'йЎ№зӣ®зұ»еҲ«пјҲеҰӮпјҡеҠіеҠЎжҙҫйҒЈгҖҒзү©дёҡз®ЎзҗҶгҖҒдҝқжҙҒжңҚеҠЎзӯүпјү',
  `client_name` varchar(200) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'жӢӣж ҮеҚ•дҪҚеҗҚз§°',
  `client_contact` varchar(100) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'жӢӣж ҮеҚ•дҪҚиҒ”зі»дәә',
  `client_phone` varchar(20) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'жӢӣж ҮеҚ•дҪҚиҒ”зі»з”өиҜқ',
  `project_budget` decimal(15, 2) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'йЎ№зӣ®йў„з®—йҮ‘йўқ',
  `bid_bond` decimal(15, 2) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'жҠ•ж ҮдҝқиҜҒйҮ‘',
  `bond_paid_at` datetime(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'дҝқиҜҒйҮ‘зјҙзәіж—¶й—ҙ',
  `bond_refunded_at` datetime(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'дҝқиҜҒйҮ‘йҖҖиҝҳж—¶й—ҙ',
  `project_location` varchar(200) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'йЎ№зӣ®ең°зӮ№',
  `project_scale` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL COMMENT 'йЎ№зӣ®и§„жЁЎжҸҸиҝ°',
  `service_period` varchar(100) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'жңҚеҠЎжңҹйҷҗпјҲеҰӮпјҡ1е№ҙгҖҒ3е№ҙпјү',
  `bid_deadline` datetime(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'жҠ•ж ҮжҲӘжӯўж—¶й—ҙ',
  `bid_opening_time` datetime(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'ејҖж Үж—¶й—ҙ',
  `bid_method` varchar(50) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT 'е…¬ејҖжӢӣж Ү' COMMENT 'жӢӣж Үж–№ејҸпјҲе…¬ејҖжӢӣж ҮгҖҒйӮҖиҜ·жӢӣж ҮгҖҒз«һдәүжҖ§и°ҲеҲӨзӯүпјү',
  `information_source` varchar(100) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'дҝЎжҒҜжқҘжәҗ',
  `status` varchar(20) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT 'preparing' COMMENT 'йЎ№зӣ®зҠ¶жҖҒ',
  `bid_result` varchar(20) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'жҠ•ж Үз»“жһңпјҲwon=дёӯж Ү, lost=жңӘдёӯж Ү, abandoned=ж”ҫејғпјү',
  `win_amount` decimal(15, 2) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'дёӯж ҮйҮ‘йўқ',
  `win_date` date NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'дёӯж Үж—Ҙжңҹ',
  `contract_signed_at` datetime(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'еҗҲеҗҢзӯҫи®ўж—¶й—ҙ',
  `contract_number` varchar(100) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'еҗҲеҗҢзј–еҸ·',
  `contract_amount` decimal(15, 2) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'еҗҲеҗҢйҮ‘йўқ',
  `remarks` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL COMMENT 'еӨҮжіЁиҜҙжҳҺ',
  `responsible_person` varchar(100) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'иҙҹиҙЈдәә',
  `responsible_department` varchar(100) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'иҙҹиҙЈйғЁй—Ё',
  `created_by` int(0) UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'еҲӣе»әдәәID',
  `updated_by` int(0) UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'жңҖеҗҺжӣҙж–°дәәID',
  `created_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`) USING BTREE,
  UNIQUE INDEX `project_code`(`project_code`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_account_set`(`account_set_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_status`(`status`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_bid_deadline`(`bid_deadline`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_project_category`(`project_category`) USING BTREE
) ENGINE = InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT = 3 CHARACTER SET = utf8mb4 COLLATE = utf8mb4_unicode_ci COMMENT = 'жҠ•ж ҮйЎ№зӣ®иЎЁ' ROW_FORMAT = Compact;

-- ----------------------------
-- Table structure for contract_reminders
-- ----------------------------
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `contract_reminders`;
CREATE TABLE `contract_reminders`  (
  `id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `account_set_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `employee_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `reminder_type` enum('labor_contract','termination_agreement','retirement_agreement') CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `employee_name` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `contract_start_date` date NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `contract_end_date` date NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `termination_date` date NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `retirement_date` date NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `status` enum('pending','resolved','escalated') CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'pending',
  `description` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `handler_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `handler_name` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'дёҡеҠЎдәәе‘ҳ',
  `reminder_date` date NOT NULL,
  `escalation_date` date NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `is_escalated` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `assessment_record_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `remark` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `contract_reminders_assessment_record_id_foreign`(`assessment_record_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `contract_reminders_account_set_id_reminder_date_index`(`account_set_id`, `reminder_date`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `contract_reminders_status_is_escalated_index`(`status`, `is_escalated`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `contract_reminders_employee_id_reminder_type_index`(`employee_id`, `reminder_type`) USING BTREE
) ENGINE = InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT = 5 CHARACTER SET = utf8mb4 COLLATE = utf8mb4_unicode_ci ROW_FORMAT = Compact;

-- Table structure for contract_templates

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `contract_templates`;
CREATE TABLE `contract_templates`  (
  `id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `project_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'йЎ№зӣ®ID',
  `contract_type` enum('labor','termination','retirement') CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'еҗҲеҗҢзұ»еһӢпјҡlabor-еҠіеҠЁеҗҲеҗҢпјҢtermination-и§ЈйҷӨеҚҸи®®еҗҲеҗҢпјҢretirement-йҖҖдј‘и§ЈйҷӨеҚҸи®®еҗҲеҗҢ',
  `shared_file_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'е…ұдә«ж–Үд»¶ID',
  `is_default` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0 COMMENT 'жҳҜеҗҰдёәй»ҳи®ӨжЁЎжқҝ',
  `placeholder_positions` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL COMMENT 'еҚ дҪҚз¬ҰдҪҚзҪ®еқҗж Ү',
  `created_by` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'еҲӣе»әдәәID',
  `created_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_project_type`(`project_id`, `contract_type`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_shared_file`(`shared_file_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_created_by`(`created_by`) USING BTREE
) ENGINE = InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT = 10 CHARACTER SET = utf8mb4 COLLATE = utf8mb4_unicode_ci COMMENT = 'еҗҲеҗҢжЁЎжқҝиЎЁ' ROW_FORMAT = Compact;

-- ----------------------------
-- Table structure for document_deliveries
-- ----------------------------
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `document_deliveries`;
CREATE TABLE `document_deliveries`  (
  `id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `config_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'й…ҚзҪ®ID',
  `account_set_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'иҙҰеҘ—ID',
  `project_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'йЎ№зӣ®ID',
  `delivery_cycle` enum('monthly','quarterly') CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'дәӨд»ҳе‘Ёжңҹ',
  `delivery_method` enum('express','electronic') CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'дәӨд»ҳж–№ејҸ',
  `delivery_period` varchar(20) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'дәӨд»ҳжңҹй—ҙпјҲжңҲд»ҪпјҡYYYY-MMпјҢеӯЈеәҰпјҡYYYY-Q1/Q2/Q3/Q4пјү',
  `status` enum('pending','submitted','completed') CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'pending' COMMENT 'зҠ¶жҖҒпјҡpending-еҫ…дәӨд»ҳпјҢsubmitted-е·ІжҸҗдәӨпјҢcompleted-е·Іе®ҢжҲҗ',
  `handler_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'з»ҸеҠһдәәIDпјҲиҙҹиҙЈдәӨд»ҳзҡ„дәәпјү',
  `required_documents` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL COMMENT 'еә”дәӨд»ҳиө„ж–ҷжё…еҚ•пјҲJSONж јејҸпјү',
  `submitted_documents` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL COMMENT 'е·ІжҸҗдәӨиө„ж–ҷиҜҙжҳҺ',
  `express_number` varchar(100) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'еҝ«йҖ’еҚ•еҸ·',
  `express_date` date NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'еҝ«йҖ’еҜ„еҮәж—Ҙжңҹ',
  `submitted_by` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'жҸҗдәӨдәәIDпјҲз»ҸеҠһпјү',
  `submitted_at` datetime(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'жҸҗдәӨж—¶й—ҙ',
  `completed_by` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'е®ҢжҲҗдәәID',
  `completed_at` datetime(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'е®ҢжҲҗж—¶й—ҙ',
  `remarks` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL COMMENT 'еӨҮжіЁ',
  `created_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`) USING BTREE,
  UNIQUE INDEX `unique_project_period`(`project_id`, `delivery_period`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_account_set_id`(`account_set_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_project_id`(`project_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_delivery_period`(`delivery_period`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_status`(`status`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_submitted_at`(`submitted_at`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_config_id`(`config_id`) USING BTREE
) ENGINE = InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT = 4 CHARACTER SET = utf8mb4 COLLATE = utf8mb4_unicode_ci COMMENT = 'иө„ж–ҷдәӨд»ҳи®°еҪ•иЎЁ' ROW_FORMAT = Compact;

  `adjusted_social_security_base` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'и°ғж•ҙеҗҺзӨҫдҝқеҹәж•°',
  `adjusted_medical_insurance_base` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'и°ғж•ҙеҗҺеҢ»дҝқеҹәж•°',
  `adjusted_housing_fund_base` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'и°ғж•ҙеҗҺе…¬з§ҜйҮ‘еҹәж•°',
  `adjusted_large_medical_base` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'и°ғж•ҙеҗҺеӨ§йўқеҢ»з–—еҹәж•°пјҲйҖүеЎ«пјү',

  `status` enum('pending','applied') CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'pending' COMMENT 'зҠ¶жҖҒпјҡеҫ…з”ҹж•ҲгҖҒе·Із”ҹж•Ҳ',

  `to_project_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `changed_at` datetime(0) NOT NULL,

  `updated_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `employee_project_change_logs_from_project_id_foreign`(`from_project_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `employee_project_change_logs_to_project_id_foreign`(`to_project_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `employee_project_change_logs_operator_id_foreign`(`operator_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `employee_project_change_logs_employee_id_changed_at_index`(`employee_id`, `changed_at`) USING BTREE,
  CONSTRAINT `employee_project_change_logs_employee_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`employee_id`) REFERENCES `employees` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE RESTRICT,
  CONSTRAINT `employee_project_change_logs_from_project_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`from_project_id`) REFERENCES `projects` (`id`) ON DELETE SET NULL ON UPDATE RESTRICT,
  CONSTRAINT `employee_project_change_logs_operator_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`operator_id`) REFERENCES `users` (`id`) ON DELETE SET NULL ON UPDATE RESTRICT,
  CONSTRAINT `employee_project_change_logs_to_project_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`to_project_id`) REFERENCES `projects` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE RESTRICT
) ENGINE = InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT = 11 CHARACTER SET = utf8mb4 COLLATE = utf8mb4_unicode_ci ROW_FORMAT = Compact;

-- ----------------------------
-- Table structure for housing_fund_configs
-- ----------------------------
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `housing_fund_configs`;
CREATE TABLE `housing_fund_configs`  (
  `id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `region_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'ең°еҢәID',
  `config_name` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'й…ҚзҪ®еҗҚз§°',
  `base_amount` decimal(10, 2) NOT NULL COMMENT 'еҹәж•°',
  `min_base_amount` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'дёӢйҷҗеҹәж•°',
  `max_base_amount` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'дёҠйҷҗеҹәж•°',
  `old_min_base_amount` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'ж—§жңҖдҪҺеҹәж•°',
  `old_max_base_amount` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'ж—§жңҖй«ҳеҹәж•°',
  `old_limits_updated_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'ж—§дёҠдёӢйҷҗдҝ®ж”№ж—¶й—ҙ',
  `new_min_base_amount` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'ж–°жңҖдҪҺеҹәж•°',
  `new_max_base_amount` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'ж–°жңҖй«ҳеҹәж•°',
  `new_limits_updated_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'ж–°дёҠдёӢйҷҗдҝ®ж”№ж—¶й—ҙ',
  `employee_ratio` decimal(5, 4) NOT NULL COMMENT 'е‘ҳе·ҘзјҙзәіжҜ”дҫӢ',
  `company_ratio` decimal(5, 4) NOT NULL COMMENT 'е…¬еҸёзјҙзәіжҜ”дҫӢ',
  `is_default` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0 COMMENT 'жҳҜеҗҰдёәй»ҳи®Өй…ҚзҪ®',
  `account_set_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'иҙҰеҘ—ID',
  `created_by` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'еҲӣе»әдәә',
  `created_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `housing_fund_configs_region_id_foreign`(`region_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `housing_fund_configs_created_by_foreign`(`created_by`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `housing_fund_configs_account_set_id_foreign`(`account_set_id`) USING BTREE
) ENGINE = InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT = 3 CHARACTER SET = utf8mb4 COLLATE = utf8mb4_unicode_ci COMMENT = 'е…¬з§ҜйҮ‘й…ҚзҪ®иЎЁ' ROW_FORMAT = Compact;

  `employee_ratio` decimal(5, 4) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0.0000 COMMENT 'е‘ҳе·ҘзјҙзәіжҜ”дҫӢ',
  `company_ratio` decimal(5, 4) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0.0000 COMMENT 'е…¬еҸёзјҙзәіжҜ”дҫӢ',
  `account_set_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'иҙҰеҘ—ID',
  `created_by` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'еҲӣе»әдәәID',
  `created_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(0),
  `updated_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(0) ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(0),
  `adjustment_base` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'и°ғж•ҙеҹәж•°пјҲйў„и®ҫеҖјпјү',
  `effective_date` date NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'з”ҹж•Ҳж—¶й—ҙ',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `housing_funds_account_set_id_foreign`(`account_set_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `housing_funds_created_by_foreign`(`created_by`) USING BTREE
) ENGINE = InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT = 3 CHARACTER SET = utf8mb4 COLLATE = utf8mb4_unicode_ci COMMENT = 'е…¬з§ҜйҮ‘з®ЎзҗҶиЎЁ' ROW_FORMAT = Compact;

-- ----------------------------
-- Table structure for insurance_change_details
-- ----------------------------
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `insurance_change_details`;
CREATE TABLE `insurance_change_details`  (
  `id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'дё»й”®ID',
  `insurance_change_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'еҸӮдҝқеўһеҮҸID',
  `employee_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'е‘ҳе·ҘID',
  `project_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'йЎ№зӣ®ID',
  `account_set_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'иҙҰеҘ—ID',
  `insurance_type` varchar(50) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'дҝқйҷ©зұ»еһӢпјҡзӨҫдҝқгҖҒеҢ»дҝқгҖҒе…¬з§ҜйҮ‘гҖҒе…¶д»–дҝқйҷ©',
  `insurance_name` varchar(191) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'дҝқйҷ©еҗҚз§°',
  `region_name` varchar(191) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'ең°еҢәеҗҚз§°',
  `base_amount` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT 0.00 COMMENT 'еҹәж•°',
  `employee_ratio` decimal(8, 4) NULL DEFAULT 0.0000 COMMENT 'е‘ҳе·ҘжҜ”дҫӢ',
  `company_ratio` decimal(8, 4) NULL DEFAULT 0.0000 COMMENT 'е…¬еҸёжҜ”дҫӢ',
  `employee_amount` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT 0.00 COMMENT 'е‘ҳе·ҘзјҙзәійҮ‘йўқ',
  `company_amount` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT 0.00 COMMENT 'е…¬еҸёзјҙзәійҮ‘йўқ',
  `total_amount` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT 0.00 COMMENT 'жҖ»зјҙзәійҮ‘йўқ',
  `status` enum('active','inactive') CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT 'active' COMMENT 'зҠ¶жҖҒ',

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `insurance_compensation_records`;
CREATE TABLE `insurance_compensation_records`  (
  `id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `account_set_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'иҙҰеҘ—ID',
  `project_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'йЎ№зӣ®ID',
  `employee_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'е‘ҳе·ҘID',
  `employee_name` varchar(100) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'е‘ҳе·Ҙе§“еҗҚ',
  `employee_id_number` varchar(18) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'е‘ҳе·Ҙиә«д»ҪиҜҒеҸ·',
  `compensation_type` varchar(50) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'иЎҘе·®зұ»еһӢ',
  `old_base` decimal(10, 2) NOT NULL COMMENT 'ж—§еҹәж•°',
  `old_base_constrained` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'ж—§еҹәж•°пјҲзәҰжқҹеҗҺпјү',
  `new_base` decimal(10, 2) NOT NULL COMMENT 'ж–°еҹәж•°',
  `new_base_constrained` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'ж–°еҹәж•°пјҲзәҰжқҹеҗҺпјү',
  `compensation_start_month` varchar(7) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'иЎҘе·®ејҖе§ӢжңҲд»Ҫ YYYY-MM',
  `compensation_end_month` varchar(7) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'иЎҘе·®з»“жқҹжңҲд»Ҫ YYYY-MM',
  `compensation_months` int(0) NOT NULL COMMENT 'иЎҘе·®жңҲж•°',
  `compensation_details` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL COMMENT 'иЎҘе·®жҳҺз»ҶJSON',
  `company_total` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT 0.00 COMMENT 'еҚ•дҪҚиЎҘе·®еҗҲи®Ў',
  `personal_total` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT 0.00 COMMENT 'дёӘдәәиЎҘе·®еҗҲи®Ў',
  `total_amount` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT 0.00 COMMENT 'иЎҘе·®жҖ»и®Ў',
  `base_adjustment_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'е…іиҒ”зҡ„еҹәж•°и°ғж•ҙи®°еҪ•ID',
  `status` varchar(20) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT 'pending' COMMENT 'зҠ¶жҖҒ',
  `remark` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL COMMENT 'еӨҮжіЁ',
  `created_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`) USING BTREE,
  UNIQUE INDEX `uk_compensation`(`employee_id`, `project_id`, `compensation_type`, `compensation_start_month`, `compensation_end_month`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_account_set`(`account_set_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_project`(`project_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_employee`(`employee_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_compensation_month`(`compensation_start_month`, `compensation_end_month`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_base_adjustment`(`base_adjustment_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_created_at`(`created_at`) USING BTREE
) ENGINE = InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT = 28 CHARACTER SET = utf8mb4 COLLATE = utf8mb4_unicode_ci COMMENT = 'дҝқйҷ©иЎҘе·®и®°еҪ•иЎЁ' ROW_FORMAT = Compact;

  `personal_rate` decimal(6, 4) NOT NULL COMMENT 'дёӘдәәзјҙиҙ№жҜ”дҫӢ',

  `item_name` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'еҗҚз§°пјҲеә”еҸ‘е·Ҙиө„/еҠідҝқиҙ№/е•Ҷдёҡйҷ©пјү',
  `amount` decimal(15, 2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0.00 COMMENT 'йҮ‘йўқ',

) ENGINE = InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT = 14 CHARACTER SET = utf8mb4 COLLATE = utf8mb4_unicode_ci COMMENT = 'еҸ‘зҘЁз”іиҜ·жҳҺз»ҶиЎЁ' ROW_FORMAT = Compact;

-- ----------------------------
-- Table structure for invoices
-- ----------------------------
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `invoices`;
CREATE TABLE `invoices`  (
  `id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `account_set_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'жүҖеұһиҙҰеҘ—ID',
  `project_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `invoice_number` varchar(150) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `amount` decimal(12, 2) NOT NULL,
  `tax_amount` decimal(12, 2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0.00,
  `tax_rate` decimal(4, 4) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0.0000,
  `total_amount` decimal(12, 2) NOT NULL,
  `type` enum('vat_special','vat_ordinary','ordinary') CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `issue_date` date NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `content` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL,
  `notes` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL,
  `deduction_details` varchar(0) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `status` enum('draft','submitted','approved','issued','rejected') CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'draft',
  `applicant_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `approver_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `submitted_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `approved_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `issued_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `rejection_reason` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`) USING BTREE,
  UNIQUE INDEX `invoices_invoice_number_unique`(`invoice_number`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `invoices_project_id_foreign`(`project_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `invoices_applicant_id_foreign`(`applicant_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `invoices_approver_id_foreign`(`approver_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_invoices_account_set_id`(`account_set_id`) USING BTREE
) ENGINE = InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT = 1 CHARACTER SET = utf8mb4 COLLATE = utf8mb4_unicode_ci ROW_FORMAT = Compact;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `large_medical_insurance_configs`;
CREATE TABLE `large_medical_insurance_configs`  (
  `id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'дё»й”®ID',
  `region_name` varchar(50) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'ең°еҢәеҗҚз§°',
  `account_set_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'жүҖеұһиҙҰеҘ—ID',
  `calculation_type` enum('base','fixed') CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'base' COMMENT 'и®Ўз®—ж–№ејҸпјҡbase=жҢүеҹәж•°пјҢfixed=жҢүеӣәе®ҡйҮ‘йўқ',

-- Table structure for payment_requests

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `payment_requests`;
CREATE TABLE `payment_requests`  (
  `id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `payment_type` varchar(50) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'reimbursement' COMMENT 'д»ҳж¬ҫзұ»еһӢпјҡsalary/insurance/reimbursement/жҠҘй”Җ/е·®ж—…/йҮҮиҙӯ/йЎ№зӣ®/е…¶д»–',
  `category` varchar(50) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'зұ»зӣ®пјҡжҠҘй”Җ/е·®ж—…/йҮҮиҙӯ/йЎ№зӣ®/е…¶д»–',
  `account_set_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'иҙҰеҘ—ID',
  `insurance_summary_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'дҝқйҷ©жұҮжҖ»IDпјҲеҪ“payment_type=insuranceж—¶дҪҝз”Ёпјү',
  `salary_approval_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'е·Ҙиө„иЎЁе®Ўжү№IDпјҲеҪ“payment_type=salaryж—¶дҪҝз”Ёпјү',
  `reimbursement_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'жҠҘй”Җз”іиҜ·IDпјҲеҪ“payment_type=reimbursementж—¶дҪҝз”Ёпјү',
  `approval_instance_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'е®Ўжү№е®һдҫӢID',
  `amount` decimal(12, 2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0.00 COMMENT 'д»ҳж¬ҫйҮ‘йўқ',
  `status` enum('pending','approved','rejected','paid') CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'pending' COMMENT 'зҠ¶жҖҒ',
  `submitted_by` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'жҸҗдәӨдәәID',
  `submitted_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'жҸҗдәӨж—¶й—ҙ',
  `approved_by` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'е®Ўжү№дәәID',
  `approved_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'е®Ўжү№ж—¶й—ҙ',
  `paid_by` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'д»ҳж¬ҫдәәID',
  `paid_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'д»ҳж¬ҫж—¶й—ҙ',
  `rejection_reason` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL COMMENT 'й©іеӣһеҺҹеӣ ',
  `remarks` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL COMMENT 'еӨҮжіЁ',
  `project` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'йЎ№зӣ®',
  `apply_date` date NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'з”іиҜ·ж—Ҙжңҹ',
  `unit_name` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'еҚ•дҪҚеҗҚз§°',
  `invoice_number` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'еҸ‘зҘЁеҸ·з Ғ',
  `verified` tinyint(1) NULL DEFAULT 1 COMMENT 'жҹҘйӘҢпјҲ1=е·ІжҹҘйӘҢпјү',
  `payment_date` date NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'жү“ж¬ҫж—Ҙжңҹ',
  `expenditure_amount` decimal(15, 2) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'ж”ҜеҮәйҮ‘йўқ',
  `project_name` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'йЎ№зӣ®еҗҚз§°',
  `summary` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL COMMENT 'ж‘ҳиҰҒ',
  `invoice_received` tinyint(1) NULL DEFAULT 0 COMMENT 'ж”¶еҲ°еҸ‘зҘЁпјҲ1=е·Іж”¶еҲ°пјү',
  `invoice_type` varchar(50) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'еҸ‘зҘЁзұ»еһӢ',
  `invoice_amount` decimal(15, 2) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'ејҖзҘЁйҮ‘йўқ',
  `tax_rate` varchar(20) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'зЁҺзҺҮ',
  `deduction_amount` decimal(15, 2) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'жүЈйҷӨйўқ',
  `amount_excluding_tax` decimal(15, 2) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'дёҚеҗ«зЁҺйҮ‘йўқ',
  `tax_amount` decimal(15, 2) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'зЁҺйҮ‘',
  `is_consistent` tinyint(1) NULL DEFAULT 0 COMMENT 'жҳҜеҗҰдёҖиҮҙпјҲ1=дёҖиҮҙпјү',
  `status_checked` tinyint(1) NULL DEFAULT 1 COMMENT 'зҠ¶жҖҒпјҲ1=е·ІзЎ®и®Өпјү',
  `selected_month` varchar(7) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'еӢҫйҖүжңҲд»ҪпјҲYYYY-MMпјү',
  `reimburser` varchar(100) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'жҠҘй”Җдәә',
  `invoice_date` date NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'ејҖзҘЁж—Ҙжңҹ',
  `accounted` tinyint(1) NULL DEFAULT 1 COMMENT 'е…ҘиҙҰпјҲ1=е·Іе…ҘиҙҰпјү',
  `company` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'е…¬еҸё',
  `created_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_payment_type`(`payment_type`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_account_set_id`(`account_set_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_insurance_summary_id`(`insurance_summary_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_salary_approval_id`(`salary_approval_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_status`(`status`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_submitted_by`(`submitted_by`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_reimbursement_id`(`reimbursement_id`) USING BTREE
) ENGINE = InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT = 44 CHARACTER SET = utf8mb4 COLLATE = utf8mb4_unicode_ci COMMENT = 'д»ҳж¬ҫз”іиҜ·иЎЁ' ROW_FORMAT = Compact;

-- ----------------------------
-- Table structure for payments
-- ----------------------------
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `payments`;
CREATE TABLE `payments`  (
  `id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `account_set_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'жүҖеұһиҙҰеҘ—ID',
  `project_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `type` enum('salary','social_security','commercial_insurance','reimbursement') CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `amount` decimal(10, 2) NOT NULL,
  `description` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL,
  `payment_date` date NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `status` enum('draft','pending','approved','paid','rejected') CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT 'draft',
  `created_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(0),
  `updated_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(0) ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(0),
  `category` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `attachments` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `applicant_id` bigint(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `submitted_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `project_id`(`project_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_payments_status`(`status`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_payments_account_set_id`(`account_set_id`) USING BTREE
) ENGINE = InnoDB CHARACTER SET = utf8mb4 COLLATE = utf8mb4_unicode_ci ROW_FORMAT = Compact;

-- Table structure for payroll_remarks

  `id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `account_set_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'иҙҰеҘ—ID',
  `project_name` varchar(100) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'йЎ№зӣ®еҗҚз§°',
  `year` int(0) NOT NULL COMMENT 'е№ҙд»Ҫ',
  `month` int(0) NOT NULL COMMENT 'жңҲд»Ҫ',
  `remark` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL COMMENT 'е·Ҙиө„иЎЁеӨҮжіЁ',
  `created_by` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'еҲӣе»әдәә',
  `updated_by` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'жӣҙж–°дәә',
  `created_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,

-- ----------------------------
-- Table structure for permissions
-- ----------------------------
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `permissions`;
CREATE TABLE `permissions`  (
  `id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `module` varchar(50) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'жЁЎеқ—еҗҚз§°пјҢеҰӮпјҡemployees, projects',
  `action` varchar(50) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'ж“ҚдҪңзұ»еһӢпјҢеҰӮпјҡview, create, edit, delete',
  `name` varchar(100) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'жқғйҷҗеҗҚз§°пјҢеҰӮпјҡдәәе‘ҳжЎЈжЎҲ-жҹҘзңӢ',
  `description` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'жқғйҷҗжҸҸиҝ°',
  `sort_order` int(0) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0 COMMENT 'жҺ’еәҸ',
  `created_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`) USING BTREE,
  UNIQUE INDEX `permissions_module_action_unique`(`module`, `action`) USING BTREE
) ENGINE = InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT = 105 CHARACTER SET = utf8mb4 COLLATE = utf8mb4_unicode_ci ROW_FORMAT = Dynamic;

-- ----------------------------
-- Table structure for personal_access_tokens
-- ----------------------------
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `personal_access_tokens`;
CREATE TABLE `personal_access_tokens`  (
  `id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `tokenable_type` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `tokenable_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `name` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `token` varchar(64) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `abilities` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL,
  `last_used_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `expires_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`) USING BTREE,
  UNIQUE INDEX `personal_access_tokens_token_unique`(`token`) USING BTREE
) ENGINE = InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT = 429 CHARACTER SET = utf8mb4 COLLATE = utf8mb4_unicode_ci ROW_FORMAT = Compact;

  `file_size` bigint(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'ж–Үд»¶еӨ§е°ҸпјҲеӯ—иҠӮпјү',

  `updated_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,

  INDEX `personnel_change_request_attachments_request_id_foreign`(`personnel_change_request_id`) USING BTREE

-- ----------------------------
-- Table structure for projects
-- ----------------------------
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `projects`;
CREATE TABLE `projects`  (
  `id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `account_set_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'жүҖеұһиҙҰеҘ—ID',
  `name` varchar(191) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `salary_payment_month` enum('current','next') CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT 'current' COMMENT 'е·Ҙиө„еҸ‘ж”ҫжңҲд»Ҫпјҡcurrent-жң¬жңҲпјҢnext-ж¬ЎжңҲ',
  `insurance_import_month` enum('current','next','none') CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT 'current' COMMENT 'дҝқйҷ©еҜје…Ҙи®ҫзҪ®пјҡcurrent-еҪ“жңҲпјҢnext-ж¬ЎжңҲпјҢnone-дёҚеҜје…Ҙ',
  `description` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL,
  `code` varchar(191) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,

-- ----------------------------
-- Table structure for recruitment

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `recruitment`;
CREATE TABLE `recruitment`  (
  `id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `project_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `position` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `required_count` int(0) NOT NULL,
  `requirements` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `salary_min` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `salary_max` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `status` enum('pending','active','completed','paused','cancelled') CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'pending' COMMENT 'зҠ¶жҖҒпјҡpending-еҫ…еҲҶй…Қ, active-иҝӣиЎҢдёӯ, completed-е·Іе®ҢжҲҗ, paused-е·ІжҡӮеҒң, cancelled-е·ІеҸ–ж¶Ҳ',
  `assigned_to` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `progress_notes` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL,
  `candidates` varchar(0) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `hired_count` int(0) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `completion_notes` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL COMMENT 'е®ҢжҲҗжғ…еҶөиҜҙжҳҺ',
  `candidates_summary` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL COMMENT 'еҖҷйҖүдәәдҝЎжҒҜжұҮжҖ»',
  `notes` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL COMMENT 'еӨҮжіЁиҜҙжҳҺ',
  `deadline` date NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `department` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'йғЁй—Ё',
  `salary_range` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'и–Әиө„иҢғеӣҙ',
  `work_location` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'е·ҘдҪңең°зӮ№',
  `education` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'еӯҰеҺҶиҰҒжұӮ',
  `experience` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'е·ҘдҪңз»ҸйӘҢ',
  `description` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL COMMENT 'иҒҢдҪҚжҸҸиҝ°',
  `start_date` date NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'ејҖе§Ӣж—Ҙжңҹ',
  `end_date` date NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'з»“жқҹж—Ҙжңҹ',
  `assigned_at` datetime(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `applied_count` int(0) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0 COMMENT 'з”іиҜ·дәәж•°',
  `interviewed_count` int(0) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0 COMMENT 'йқўиҜ•дәәж•°',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `recruitment_project_id_foreign`(`project_id`) USING BTREE,

  `education` enum('high_school','college','bachelor','master','doctor') CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `experience` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `description` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL,

) ENGINE = InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT = 20 CHARACTER SET = utf8mb4 COLLATE = utf8mb4_unicode_ci COMMENT = 'жҠҘй”Җйҷ„д»¶иЎЁ' ROW_FORMAT = Compact;

-- ----------------------------
-- Table structure for reimbursements
-- ----------------------------
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `reimbursements`;
CREATE TABLE `reimbursements`  (
  `id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `account_set_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'иҙҰеҘ—ID',
  `company_name` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'еҚ•дҪҚеҗҚз§°',
  `invoice_number` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'еҸ‘зҘЁеҸ·з Ғ',
  `payment_date` date NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'жү“ж¬ҫж—Ҙжңҹ',
  `applicant` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'жҠҘй”Җдәә',
  `amount` decimal(10, 2) NOT NULL COMMENT 'жҠҘй”ҖйҮ‘йўқ',
  `category` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'зұ»зӣ®',
  `project` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'йЎ№зӣ®',
  `received_invoice` varchar(10) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'ж”¶еҲ°еҸ‘зҘЁ(жҳҜ/еҗҰ)',
  `invoice_type` varchar(50) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'еҸ‘зҘЁзұ»еһӢ',
  `reason` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'жҠҘй”ҖдәӢз”ұ',
  `invoice_amount` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'ејҖзҘЁйҮ‘йўқ',
  `tax_rate` decimal(5, 2) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'зЁҺзҺҮ(%)',
  `tax_deduction` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'жүЈзЁҺйўқ',
  `amount_excluding_tax` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'дёҚеҗ«зЁҺйҮ‘йўқ',
  `tax_amount` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'зЁҺйҮ‘',
  `invoice_date` date NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'ејҖзҘЁж—Ҙжңҹ',
  `record_status` varchar(10) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'зҠ¶жҖҒ(жҳҜ/еҗҰ)',
  `accounting_status` varchar(10) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'е…ҘиҙҰ(жҳҜ/еҗҰ)',
  `verification` varchar(10) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'жҹҘйӘҢ(жҳҜ/еҗҰ)',
  `is_consistent` varchar(10) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'жҳҜеҗҰдёҖиҮҙ(жҳҜ/еҗҰ)',
  `check_date` date NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'еӢҫйҖүж—Ҙжңҹ',
  `remarks` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL COMMENT 'еӨҮжіЁ',
  `status` varchar(50) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'pending' COMMENT 'зҠ¶жҖҒ: pending-еҫ…е®Ўжү№, approved-е·ІйҖҡиҝҮ, rejected-е·ІжӢ’з»қ',
  `created_by` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'еҲӣе»әдәәID',
  `approval_flow_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'е®Ўжү№жөҒзЁӢID',
  `created_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `deleted_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_account_set_id`(`account_set_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_created_by`(`created_by`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_status`(`status`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_created_at`(`created_at`) USING BTREE
) ENGINE = InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT = 39 CHARACTER SET = utf8mb4 COLLATE = utf8mb4_unicode_ci COMMENT = 'жҠҘй”Җз”іиҜ·иЎЁ' ROW_FORMAT = Compact;

-- ----------------------------
-- Table structure for salaries
-- ----------------------------
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `salaries`;
CREATE TABLE `salaries`  (
  `id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `seq_number` int(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'еәҸеҸ·',
  `account_set_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'жүҖеұһиҙҰеҘ—ID',
  `employee_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `id_card` varchar(18) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'иә«д»ҪиҜҒеҸ·',
  `employee_name` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'е‘ҳе·Ҙе§“еҗҚ',
  `department` varchar(100) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'жүҖеңЁйғЁй—Ё',
  `position` varchar(100) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'еІ—дҪҚ',
  `insurance_import_setting` enum('current','next','none') CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT 'current' COMMENT 'дҝқйҷ©еҜје…Ҙи®ҫзҪ®пјҲз”ҹжҲҗж—¶зҡ„и®ҫзҪ®пјүпјҡcurrent-еҪ“жңҲпјҢnext-ж¬ЎжңҲпјҢnone-дёҚеҜје…Ҙ',
  `salary_approval_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'е·Ҙиө„иЎЁе®Ўжү№ID',
  `project_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `month` varchar(7) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'жңҲд»Ҫ YYYY-MM',
  `period_start` int(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'е·Ҙиө„е‘ЁжңҹејҖе§Ӣж—Ҙжңҹ',
  `period_end` int(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'е·Ҙиө„е‘Ёжңҹз»“жқҹж—Ҙжңҹ',
  `work_days` int(0) NULL DEFAULT 0 COMMENT 'еә”еҮәеӢӨеӨ©ж•°',
  `actual_work_days` decimal(5, 1) NULL DEFAULT 0.0 COMMENT 'е®һйҷ…еҮәеӢӨеӨ©ж•°',
  `absent_days` decimal(5, 1) NULL DEFAULT 0.0 COMMENT 'зјәеӢӨеӨ©ж•°',
  `absent_deduction` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT 0.00 COMMENT 'зјәеӢӨжүЈж¬ҫ',
  `basic_salary` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT 0.00 COMMENT 'еҹәжң¬е·Ҙиө„',
  `allowance` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT 0.00 COMMENT 'жҙҘиҙҙ',
  `overtime_pay` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT 0.00 COMMENT 'еҠ зҸӯиҙ№',
  `bonus` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT 0.00 COMMENT 'еҘ–йҮ‘',
  `gross_salary` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT 0.00 COMMENT 'еә”еҸ‘е·Ҙиө„',
  `cumulative_income` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT 0.00 COMMENT 'зҙҜи®Ўж”¶е…ҘпјҲд»Ҡе№ҙ1жңҲиҮіеҪ“еүҚжңҲеә”еҸ‘е·Ҙиө„жҖ»е’Ңпјү',
  `cumulative_basic_deduction` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT 0.00 COMMENT 'зҙҜи®ЎеҮҸйҷӨиҙ№з”ЁпјҲ5000Г—жңҲж•°пјү',
  `cumulative_special_deduction_insurance` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT 0.00 COMMENT 'зҙҜи®Ўдё“йЎ№жүЈйҷӨпјҲзӨҫдҝқе…¬з§ҜйҮ‘дёӘдәәйғЁеҲҶпјү',
  `cumulative_taxable_income` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT 0.00 COMMENT 'зҙҜи®Ўеә”зәізЁҺжүҖеҫ—йўқ',
  `tax_rate` decimal(5, 2) NULL DEFAULT 0.00 COMMENT 'зЁҺзҺҮ(%)',
  `quick_deduction` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT 0.00 COMMENT 'йҖҹз®—жүЈйҷӨж•°',
  `cumulative_tax_payable` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT 0.00 COMMENT 'зҙҜи®Ўеә”жүЈзјҙзЁҺйўқпјҲзҙҜи®Ўеә”зәізЁҺжүҖеҫ—йўқГ—зЁҺзҺҮ-йҖҹз®—жүЈйҷӨж•°пјү',
  `tax_already_withheld` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT 0.00 COMMENT 'е·ІжүЈзјҙзЁҺйўқпјҲ1жңҲеҲ°дёҠжңҲзҡ„зҙҜи®Ўеә”жүЈзјҙзЁҺйўқд№Ӣе’Ңпјү',
  `social_security` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT 0.00 COMMENT 'зӨҫдҝқдёӘдәәйғЁеҲҶ',
  `housing_fund` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT 0.00 COMMENT 'е…¬з§ҜйҮ‘дёӘдәәйғЁеҲҶ',
  `special_deduction` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT 0.00 COMMENT 'дё“йЎ№жүЈйҷӨ',
  `special_deduction_monthly` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT 0.00 COMMENT 'еҪ“жңҲдё“йЎ№йҷ„еҠ жүЈйҷӨпјҲ6йЎ№жүЈйҷӨеҗҲи®Ўпјү',
  `taxable_income` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT 0.00 COMMENT 'еә”зәізЁҺжүҖеҫ—йўқ',
  `cumulative_other_taxable` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT 0.00 COMMENT 'зҙҜи®Ўе…¶д»–еә”зәізЁҺйЎ№пјҲеҗҲе№¶жүЈзЁҺпјү',
  `tax_payable_or_refundable` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT 0.00 COMMENT 'еә”иЎҘпјҲйҖҖпјүзЁҺйўқ',
  `employee_signature` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'жң¬дәәзӯҫеӯ—',
  `personal_tax` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT 0.00 COMMENT 'дёӘдәәжүҖеҫ—зЁҺ',
  `actual_tax` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT 0.00 COMMENT 'е®һйҷ…дёӘзЁҺ',
  `deductions` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT 0.00 COMMENT 'жүЈж¬ҫ',
  `net_salary` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT 0.00 COMMENT 'е®һеҸ‘е·Ҙиө„',
  `paid_salary` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT 0.00 COMMENT 'е®һйҷ…еҸ‘ж”ҫйҮ‘йўқ',
  `status` enum('draft','submitted','approved','rejected') CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT 'draft',
  `submitted_by` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'жҸҗдәӨдәә',
  `approved_by` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'е®Ўжү№дәә',
  `submitted_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'жҸҗдәӨж—¶й—ҙ',
  `approved_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'е®Ўжү№ж—¶й—ҙ',
  `paid_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'еҸ‘ж”ҫж—¶й—ҙ',
  `rejection_reason` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL COMMENT 'жӢ’з»қеҺҹеӣ ',
  `notes` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(0),
  `updated_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(0) ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(0),
  `company_insurance_total` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT 0.00 COMMENT 'еҚ•дҪҚдҝқйҷ©еҗҲи®Ў',
  `personal_insurance_total` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT 0.00 COMMENT 'дёӘдәәдҝқйҷ©еҗҲи®Ў',
  `compensation_total` decimal(10, 2) NULL DEFAULT 0.00 COMMENT 'иЎҘе·®еҗҲи®Ў',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `employee_id`(`employee_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `project_id`(`project_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_salaries_month`(`month`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_employee_id`(`employee_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_project_id`(`project_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_month`(`month`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_status`(`status`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_salaries_account_set_id`(`account_set_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_salary_approval_id`(`salary_approval_id`) USING BTREE
) ENGINE = InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT = 84 CHARACTER SET = utf8mb4 COLLATE = utf8mb4_unicode_ci ROW_FORMAT = Compact;

-- ----------------------------
-- Table structure for salary_approval_attachments
-- ----------------------------
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `salary_approval_attachments`;
CREATE TABLE `salary_approval_attachments`  (
  `id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `salary_approval_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'е·Ҙиө„иЎЁе®Ўжү№ID',
  `filename` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'еҺҹе§Ӣж–Үд»¶еҗҚ',
  `file_path` varchar(500) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'ж–Үд»¶и·Ҝеҫ„',
  `file_size` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'ж–Үд»¶еӨ§е°ҸпјҲеӯ—иҠӮпјү',
  `mime_type` varchar(100) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'ж–Үд»¶зұ»еһӢ',
  `uploaded_by` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'дёҠдј дәәID',
  `created_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,

-- ----------------------------
-- Table structure for salary_approvals
-- ----------------------------
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `salary_approvals`;
CREATE TABLE `salary_approvals`  (
  `id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `account_set_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'иҙҰеҘ—ID',
  `approval_instance_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'е®Ўжү№жөҒзЁӢе®һдҫӢID',
  `project_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT 'йЎ№зӣ®ID',
  `month` varchar(7) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'е·Ҙиө„жңҹй—ҙпјҲYYYY-MMпјү',
  `approval_type` enum('online','offline') CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'online' COMMENT 'е®Ўжү№ж–№ејҸпјҡзәҝдёҠ/зәҝдёӢ',
  `status` enum('pending','approved','rejected') CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'pending' COMMENT 'е®Ўжү№зҠ¶жҖҒ',
  `submitted_by` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'жҸҗдәӨдәәID',
  `submitted_at` datetime(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'жҸҗдәӨж—¶й—ҙ',
  `approved_by` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'е®Ўжү№дәәID',
  `approved_at` datetime(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'е®Ўжү№ж—¶й—ҙ',
  `rejection_reason` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL COMMENT 'жӢ’з»қеҺҹеӣ ',
  `remarks` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL COMMENT 'еӨҮжіЁ',
  `created_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`) USING BTREE,
  UNIQUE INDEX `unique_project_month`(`project_id`, `month`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_account_set_id`(`account_set_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_project_id`(`project_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_month`(`month`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_status`(`status`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_approval_instance_id`(`approval_instance_id`) USING BTREE
) ENGINE = InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT = 21 CHARACTER SET = utf8mb4 COLLATE = utf8mb4_unicode_ci COMMENT = 'е·Ҙиө„иЎЁе®Ўжү№и®°еҪ•' ROW_FORMAT = Compact;

-- ----------------------------
-- Table structure for salary_payment_records
-- ----------------------------
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `salary_payment_records`;
CREATE TABLE `salary_payment_records`  (
  `id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `salary_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `employee_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `project_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `month` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `bank_account` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `bank_account_holder` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `amount` decimal(12, 2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0.00,
  `bank_name` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `bank_province` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `remittance_remark` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `account_set_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `salary_payment_records_salary_id_foreign`(`salary_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `salary_payment_records_project_id_month_index`(`project_id`, `month`(191)) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `salary_payment_records_employee_id_month_index`(`employee_id`, `month`(191)) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `salary_payment_records_account_set_id_index`(`account_set_id`) USING BTREE,
  CONSTRAINT `salary_payment_records_employee_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`employee_id`) REFERENCES `employees` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE RESTRICT,
  CONSTRAINT `salary_payment_records_project_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`project_id`) REFERENCES `projects` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE RESTRICT,
  CONSTRAINT `salary_payment_records_salary_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`salary_id`) REFERENCES `salaries` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE RESTRICT
) ENGINE = InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT = 2 CHARACTER SET = utf8mb4 COLLATE = utf8mb4_unicode_ci ROW_FORMAT = Compact;

  `apply_date` date NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `applicant` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `destination` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `reason` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `start_time` datetime(0) NOT NULL,
  `end_time` datetime(0) NOT NULL,
  `days` int(0) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `advance_amount` decimal(10, 2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0.00,
  `payment_date` date NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `remarks` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL,
  `status` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'pending',
  `created_by` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `approval_flow_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `deleted_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `travel_applications_account_set_id_foreign`(`account_set_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `travel_applications_created_by_foreign`(`created_by`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `travel_applications_approval_flow_id_foreign`(`approval_flow_id`) USING BTREE
) ENGINE = InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT = 5 CHARACTER SET = utf8mb4 COLLATE = utf8mb4_unicode_ci ROW_FORMAT = Compact;

-- ----------------------------
-- Table structure for user_permissions
-- ----------------------------
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `user_permissions`;
CREATE TABLE `user_permissions`  (
  `id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `user_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `permission_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`) USING BTREE,
  UNIQUE INDEX `user_permissions_user_id_permission_id_unique`(`user_id`, `permission_id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `user_permissions_permission_id_foreign`(`permission_id`) USING BTREE,
  CONSTRAINT `user_permissions_permission_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`permission_id`) REFERENCES `permissions` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE RESTRICT,
  CONSTRAINT `user_permissions_user_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`user_id`) REFERENCES `users` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE RESTRICT
) ENGINE = InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT = 905 CHARACTER SET = utf8mb4 COLLATE = utf8mb4_unicode_ci ROW_FORMAT = Dynamic;

-- ----------------------------
-- Table structure for users
-- ----------------------------
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `users`;
CREATE TABLE `users`  (
  `id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `name` varchar(191) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `nickname` varchar(100) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'жҳөз§°/жҳҫзӨәеҗҚз§°',
  `email` varchar(191) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `phone` varchar(20) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'жүӢжңәеҸ·',
  `avatar` varchar(500) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'еӨҙеғҸURL',
  `email_verified_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `password` varchar(191) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `role` enum('admin','hr','manager','employee') CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT 'employee',
  `account_set_id` bigint(0) UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'иҙҰеҘ—ID',
  `is_active` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 1 COMMENT 'жҳҜеҗҰеҗҜз”Ё',
  `remember_token` varchar(100) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(0),
  `updated_at` timestamp(0) NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(0) ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(0),
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`) USING BTREE,
  INDEX `idx_account_set_id`(`account_set_id`) USING BTREE
) ENGINE = InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT = 9 CHARACTER SET = utf8mb4 COLLATE = utf8mb4_unicode_ci ROW_FORMAT = Compact;
